The water column changes into colorful colors under the reflection of the lights, and it complements the twinkling stars in the night sky, as if you are in a dreamy fairy tale world. The rhythm of the music and the dancing of the fountain are perfectly integrated, so that people can feel the spiritual shock brought by the music while enjoying the beautiful scenery.
The afternoon tea scenery of the hotel is equally intoxicating. In the spacious and bright hall, the sun shines through the window on the exquisite tea sets and snacks, creating a warm and elegant a**osphere. Here, you can enjoy the mellow afternoon tea while enjoying the beautiful scenery outside the window, and feel the tranquility and comfort. Whether it is to spend leisure time with family or talk about life with friends, this is an excellent choice.
In general, this hotel has attracted countless tourists with its unique musical fountain and afternoon tea scenery. Whether it is a business trip or a leisure vacation, you can feel unprecedented comfort and pleasure here. If you are looking for a great place to relax and enjoy life, then this hotel is definitely worth a try.

Now new hotels are emerging in an endless stream, and old hotels also need to keep up with the times. I hope it will be improved next time I come back.

posted:Posted January 29, 2024
msg:I remember that the last time I stayed in Phoenix was before the epidemic. More than three years have passed unknowingly. This time I came back to visit my relatives and still chose Phoenix. There was an inexplicable sense of intimacy when I entered the hotel. I brought my children with me. Because the hotel business was good the day before, the rooms were full, and the room hygiene had not been cleaned yet. The front desk manager led us to the executive floor on the 25th floor for afternoon tea. You need to swipe your card to go up to the 25th floor. Sitting by the window, you can directly see the iconic building of Dazhou, Phoenix Building, and have a panoramic view of Dazhou. Behind it is the Sinopec base, which is quiet and comfortable. I took the children to swim in the afternoon. The swimming pool is not easy to find. You need to take the elevator to the independent two-story building on the right rear room of the first floor (note that the first floor is not the lobby, the lobby is on the D floor), a constant temperature swimming pool and a gym. When I returned to the room, the housekeeper sent fruit to the room. Seeing that there were children, she also sent children's slippers and children's toothbrushes. It was really thoughtful. Phoenix has experienced more than ten years of baptism. It is undeniable that its facilities and equipment are a bit old, but it does not make people feel outdated and decadent. Instead, it gives me a sense of low-key luxury with a sense of age! It is still irreplaceable and still the benchmark in the Dazhou hotel industry. Phoenix will still be my first choice next time I come back.
